[stdout] commit 6cf02b953eb786809e75e20b9f556e4791b2eabe
[stdout] Author: Florian Hahn <florian.hahn@arm.com>
[stdout] Date:   Tue Nov 7 16:45:48 2017 +0000
[stdout] 
[stdout]     [AArch64][SVE] Asm: Add SVE (Z) Register definitions and parsing support
[stdout]     
[stdout]     Patch [3/5] in a series to add assembler/disassembler support for AArch64 SVE unpredicated ADD/SUB instructions.
[stdout]     
[stdout]     To summarise, this patch adds:
[stdout]     
[stdout]      * SVE register definitions
[stdout]      * Methods to parse SVE register operands
[stdout]      * Methods to print SVE register operands
[stdout]      * RegKind SVEDataVector to distinguish it from other data types like scalar register or Neon vector.
[stdout]      * k_SVEDataRegister and SVEDataRegOp to describe SVE registers (which will be extended by further patches with e.g. ElementWidth and the shift-extend type).
[stdout]     
[stdout]     
[stdout]     Patch by Sander De Smalen.
[stdout]     
[stdout]     Reviewed by: rengolin
[stdout]     
[stdout]     Differential Revision: https://reviews.llvm.org/D39089
[stdout]     
[stdout]     
[stdout]     git-svn-id: https://llvm.org/svn/llvm-project/llvm/trunk@317590 91177308-0d34-0410-b5e6-96231b3b80d8

[stdout] libcxxabi log:
[stdout] commit 05ba3281482304ae8de31123a594972a495da06d
[stdout] Author: Eric Fiselier <eric@efcs.ca>
[stdout] Date:   Thu Sep 14 22:37:34 2017 +0000
[stdout] 
[stdout]     Fix ASAN build with older compiler-rt versions.
[stdout]     
[stdout]     compiler-rt recently added the __asan_handle_no_return() function that libc++abi
[stdout]     needs to use, however older versions of compiler-rt don't declare this interface
[stdout]     publicly and that breaks the libc++abi build.
[stdout]     
[stdout]     This patch attempts to fix the issues by declaring the asan function explicitly,
[stdout]     so we don't depend on compiler-rt to provide the declaration.
[stdout]     
[stdout]     git-svn-id: https://llvm.org/svn/llvm-project/libcxxabi/trunk@313308 91177308-0d34-0410-b5e6-96231b3b80d8
[stdout]
